Perfume essential oils are the key determinants of a fragrance's scent and can offer exquisite experiences for users.\n2.Perfume essential oils have been around since ancient Egypt and have long been a luxury reserved for royal elites. But in recent years, perfume essential oils have seen significant development and diversification, with research leading to a variety of different scents. With many outstanding advantages, this product has become a popular choice not only for women but also for men who appreciate it.\n\n3.The Difference Between Perfume Essential Oils and Synthetic Perfumes Because both serve the purpose of creating fragrance, it's easy to confuse perfume essential oils with synthetic perfumes. However, in reality, perfume essential oils and synthetic perfumes are entirely different and have their own characteristics.\n\n4.Alcohol Content A fundamental difference between these two lies in the alcohol content. Alcohol is considered a crucial element in creating the fragrance variations in synthetic perfumes, with alcohol making up as much as 50% to 70% of a perfume bottle. In contrast, perfume essential oils contain very little or even no alcohol. Instead, oils like Jojoba or grapeseed oil are often used to create various scents in essential oils. This also makes essential oil perfumes safer and suitable for sensitive skin areas.\n5.Fragrance The scents of perfume essential oils and synthetic perfumes do not differ significantly, especially when they are produced from similar ingredients. Therefore, it's normal for two people using the same essential oil perfume to have slightly different scents.\n\n6.Longevity Another aspect to distinguish between these products is their fragrance longevity. Regular synthetic perfumes typically consist of distilled water, essential oils, and alcohol, while essential oil perfumes only contain distilled water and essential oils without alcohol. This results in essential oil perfumes having a higher concentration of essential oils, typically 5 to 10 times more than synthetic perfumes. Consequently, essential oil perfumes have a stronger and longer-lasting scent compared to synthetic perfumes.\nIn the hierarchy of fragrances, Perfume is considered the highest and most valuable category. The longevity of Perfume fragrances usually ranges from 8 to 12 hours after application. In contrast, the average fragrance lifespan of essential oil perfumes can extend to 10 to 12 hours, or even longer. B\u1eb1ng c\u00e1ch cung c\u1ea5p ti\u1ec1n v\u00e0 t\u00e0i s\u1ea3n s\u1ed1 c\u1ee7a h\u1ecd v\u00e0o h\u1ec7 th\u1ed1ng, h\u1ecd gi\u00fap \u0111\u1ea3m b\u1ea3o r\u1eb1ng ng\u01b0\u1eddi kh\u00e1c c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 mua v\u00e0 b\u00e1n t\u00e0i s\u1ea3n n\u00e0y m\u1ed9t c\u00e1ch d\u1ec5 d\u00e0ng v\u00e0 v\u1edbi gi\u00e1 g\u1ea7n nh\u01b0 th\u1ecb tr\u01b0\u1eddng. Trong qu\u00e1 tr\u00ecnh cung c\u1ea5p thanh kho\u1ea3n, h\u1ecd c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 nh\u1eadn \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c l\u1ee3i su\u1ea5t ho\u1eb7c ph\u00ed giao d\u1ecbch t\u1eeb s\u00e0n ho\u1eb7c h\u1ed3 b\u01a1i.\ud83e\udd7d\n\n2. \u2696\ufe0fLiquidity Pool (H\u1ed3 b\u01a1i thanh kho\u1ea3n): #LP c\u0169ng c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 \u00e1m ch\u1ec9 m\u1ed9t ph\u1ea7n c\u1ee7a m\u1ed9t s\u00e0n giao d\u1ecbch ho\u1eb7c d\u1ef1 \u00e1n #DeFi (Decentralized Finance) n\u01a1i ti\u1ec1n v\u00e0 t\u00e0i s\u1ea3n s\u1ed1 \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c gom l\u1ea1i \u0111\u1ec3 t\u1ea1o ra m\u1ed9t ngu\u1ed3n cung c\u1ea5p thanh kho\u1ea3n cho c\u00e1c c\u1eb7p giao d\u1ecbch. Trong m\u1ed9t h\u1ed3 b\u01a1i thanh kho\u1ea3n, c\u00e1c nh\u00e0 cung c\u1ea5p thanh kho\u1ea3n g\u1eedi ti\u1ec1n v\u00e0 t\u00e0i s\u1ea3n s\u1ed1 c\u1ee7a h\u1ecd v\u00e0o m\u1ed9t h\u1ec7 th\u1ed1ng th\u00f4ng qua m\u1ed9t giao th\u1ee9c DeFi. H\u1ecd nh\u1eadn \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c m\u1ed9t s\u1ed1 l\u01b0\u1ee3ng token m\u1edbi \u0111\u1ea1i di\u1ec7n cho h\u1ecd trong h\u1ed3 b\u01a1i v\u00e0 c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 nh\u1eadn \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c l\u1ee3i su\u1ea5t ho\u1eb7c ph\u00ed giao d\u1ecbch t\u1eeb vi\u1ec7c tham gia v\u00e0o h\u1ed3 b\u01a1i n\u00e0y.- S\u1ef1 hi\u1ec7n di\u1ec7n c\u1ee7a LP v\u00e0 h\u1ed3 b\u01a1i thanh kho\u1ea3n l\u00e0 quan tr\u1ecdng \u0111\u1ec3 \u0111\u1ea3m b\u1ea3o t\u00ednh thanh kho\u1ea3n v\u00e0 t\u00ednh \u0111a d\u1ea1ng c\u1ee7a th\u1ecb tr\u01b0\u1eddng ti\u1ec1n \u0111i\u1ec7n t\u1eed v\u00e0 #DeFi.\n\n\ud83c\udf15 VD: Add c\u1eb7p thanh kho\u1ea3n $ETH/ $USDC\n\n\ud83c\udd98Vi\u1ec7c cung c\u1ea5p thanh kho\u1ea3n (LP) trong h\u1ed3 b\u01a1i thanh kho\u1ea3n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 ma#ng l\u1ea1i l\u1ee3i nhu\u1eadn trong m\u1ed9t s\u1ed1 tr\u01b0\u1eddng h\u1ee3p, nh\u01b0ng n\u00f3 c\u0169ng \u0111i k\u00e8m v\u1edbi r\u1ee7i ro v\u00e0 c\u1ea7n ph\u1ea3i \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c hi\u1ec3u r\u00f5 tr\u01b0\u1edbc khi b\u1ea1n quy\u1ebft \u0111\u1ecbnh tham gia. D\u01b0\u1edbi \u0111\u00e2y l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t s\u1ed1 \u0111i\u1ec1u c\u1ea7n xem x\u00e9t:\n\n\ud83d\udc49L\u1ee3i su\u1ea5t LP: Cung c\u1ea5p thanh kho\u1ea3n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 \u0111em l\u1ea1i l\u1ee3i su\u1ea5t t\u1eeb ph\u00ed giao d\u1ecbch v\u00e0 l\u1ee3i su\u1ea5t t\u1eeb h\u1ed3 b\u01a1i thanh kho\u1ea3n. Tuy nhi\u00ean, m\u1ee9c l\u1ee3i su\u1ea5t n\u00e0y c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 bi\u1ebfn \u0111\u1ed5i v\u00e0 ph\u1ee5 thu\u1ed9c v\u00e0o th\u1ecb tr\u01b0\u1eddng, d\u1ef1 \u00e1n c\u1ee5 th\u1ec3 v\u00e0 h\u1ec7 th\u1ed1ng giao d\u1ecbch. N\u00f3 kh\u00f4ng ph\u1ea3i l\u00fac n\u00e0o c\u0169ng \u0111\u1ea3m b\u1ea3o sinh l\u1eddi.\n\n\ud83d\udc49R\u1ee7i ro: LP c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 ph\u1ea3i \u0111\u1ed1i m\u1eb7t v\u1edbi r\u1ee7i ro th\u1ea5t tho\u00e1t v\u1ed1n khi gi\u00e1 c\u1ee7a m\u1ed9t s\u1ed1 t\u00e0i s\u1ea3n trong h\u1ed3 b\u01a1i thay \u0111\u1ed5i. N\u1ebfu gi\u00e1 gi\u1ea3m s\u00e2u v\u00e0 b\u1ea1n kh\u00f4ng th\u00e1o v\u1ed1n \u0111\u00fang l\u00fac, b\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 m\u1ea5t m\u1ed9t ph\u1ea7n ho\u1eb7c to\u00e0n b\u1ed9 v\u1ed1n c\u1ee7a m\u00ecnh.\n\n\ud83d\udc49Impermanent Loss: \u0110\u00e2y l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t r\u1ee7i ro \u0111\u1eb7c bi\u1ec7t li\u00ean quan \u0111\u1ebfn vi\u1ec7c cung c\u1ea5p thanh kho\u1ea3n. N\u1ebfu t\u1ef7 l\u1ec7 gi\u00e1 gi\u1eefa hai t\u00e0i s\u1ea3n trong h\u1ed3 b\u01a1i thay \u0111\u1ed5i m\u1ea1nh, b\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 g\u00e1nh ch\u1ecbu m\u1ea5t l\u1ee3i nhu\u1eadn so v\u1edbi vi\u1ec7c gi\u1eef t\u00e0i s\u1ea3n theo c\u00e1 nh\u00e2n.\n\n\ud83d\udc49Nghi\u00ean c\u1ee9u: Tr\u01b0\u1edbc khi tham gia LP, b\u1ea1n n\u00ean nghi\u00ean c\u1ee9u k\u1ef9 v\u1ec1 d\u1ef1 \u00e1n ho\u1eb7c s\u00e0n giao d\u1ecbch c\u1ee5 th\u1ec3, v\u1ec1 c\u00e1ch ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng c\u1ee7a h\u1ed3 b\u01a1i thanh kho\u1ea3n, v\u00e0 v\u1ec1 c\u00e1ch qu\u1ea3n l\u00fd r\u1ee7i ro.\n\n\ud83d\udc49B\u1ea3o m\u1eadt: B\u1ea3o v\u1ec7 an to\u00e0n t\u00e0i s\u1ea3n c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n r\u1ea5t quan tr\u1ecdng.
